import groovy.json.JsonSlurper

def failureMessage = ""


if(prev.isSuccessful()){
try {
def response = new JsonSlurper().parseText(prev.getResponseDataAsString())
if(response.BLA-BLA-BLA[0].id.toString() != vars.get("SOME_ID_TO_BE_CHEKED")){
failureMessage += "Sample name: " + prev.getSampleLabel().toString() + "\n" ;
failureMessage += "Deal ID is not in response: " + vars.get("SOME_ID_TO_BE_CHEKED") + "\n" ;
failureMessage += "RESPONSE MESSAGE: " + prev.getResponseDataAsString() + "\n";
println "ERROR: \n" + failureMessage
AssertionResult.setFailureMessage(failureMessage);
AssertionResult.setFailure(true);
}
}
catch(Exception e) { //In case if response is not JSON
println("Exception: ${e}")
failureMessage += "Sample name: " + prev.getSampleLabel().toString() + "\n" ;
failureMessage += "RESPONSE MESSAGE: " + prev.getResponseDataAsString() + "\n";
println "ERROR: \n" + failureMessage
AssertionResult.setFailureMessage(failureMessage);
AssertionResult.setFailure(true);

}
}
